         <section class="body">
          <div class="figure_block feature" data-parade-clicks="false" data-parade-location-ids="featured-image" data-parade-location-types="media" data-parade-mouseovers="false" data-parade-touches="false" data-parade-type="media" data-parade-views="false">
           <figure>
            <a href="http://communitytable.parade.com/308511/frozen_promo-2/">
             <img alt="frozen_promo" class="addthis_shareable" data-parade-image="" data-parade-image-placeholding="" src="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/frozen_promo1.png"/>
            </a>
           </figure>
          </div>
          <span data-parade-clicks="false" data-parade-location-ids="article" data-parade-location-types="promoarea" data-parade-mouseovers="false" data-parade-touches="false" data-parade-type="promoarea" data-parade-views="false">
           <p class="first">
            <em>
             <span style="line-height: 1.5em">
              Frozen is the top grossing animated film of all time and the #1 most popular party for little girls. When it came time to create my own daughters party I knew right away I was going to have to let it go and get frosty right along with everyone else!
             </span>
            </em>
           </p>
           <p>
            <span style="line-height: 1.5em">
             When planning a party with the current most popular theme, you have to really think out of the ice box to come up with something different. I love seeing how all the beautiful parties out there, many of them created by own very creative friends. Ive rounded up some great ideas for you!
            </span>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             We all know it starts with the invitation
            </strong>
           </p>
           <div class="figure_block size-100 aligncenter">
            <figure>
             <a href="http://communitytable.parade.com/308489/frozen1/">
              <img alt="Credits Left to Right " class="addthis_shareable at_include" data-parade-image="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/frozen1.jpg" data-parade-image-inlining="" data-parade-image-placeholding="true" src="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/themes/wp-theme/img/misc/tiny.gif"/>
             </a>
            </figure>
            <figcaption>
             <span class="arrow">
             </span>
             Credits Left to Right
             <span class="credit">
              (Credits Left to Right )
             </span>
            </figcaption>
           </div>
           <p>
            1. Made by a Princess 
            <a href="http://www.partiesinstyle.com/Frozen-Inspired-Printable-Birthday-Invitation-Original-Design_p_674.html" target="_blank">
             Elsa inspired invitation
            </a>
            <br/>
            2. Gemini Celebrations 
            <a href="https://www.etsy.com/shop/GeminiCelebrations" target="_blank">
             Snowflake die cut invitation
            </a>
            <br/>
            3. Squared Party Printables 
            <a href="https://www.etsy.com/listing/181291489/frozen-invitation-printable-ice-princess?ref=shop_home_feat_3" target="_blank">
             Ice Princess invitation
            </a>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             Setting the table is one of my favorite parts of the party. Everyone gathers around the food table so it has to be pretty!
            </strong>
           </p>
           <div class="figure_block size-100 aligncenter">
            <figure>
             <a href="http://communitytable.parade.com/308491/frozen2/">
              <img alt="Credits from Left to Right" class="addthis_shareable at_include" data-parade-image="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/frozen2.png" data-parade-image-inlining="" data-parade-image-placeholding="true" src="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/themes/wp-theme/img/misc/tiny.gif"/>
             </a>
            </figure>
            <figcaption>
             <span class="arrow">
             </span>
             Credits from Left to Right
            </figcaption>
           </div>
           <p>
            1.
            <a href="http://www.madebyaprincessblog.com/2014/05/Frozen-Birthday-Party.html#axzz34HbU5uQ2" target="_blank">
             Made by a Princess
            </a>
             A party completely inspired by Elsa and her ice castle.
            <br/>
            2.
            <a href="http://lauraslittlepartysite.blogspot.com/2014/03/frozen-dvd-kick-off-party.html" target="_blank">
             LAURAS little PARTY
            </a>
             Love is an Open Door party to celebrate the DVD release.
            <br/>
            3.
            <a href="http://www.greygreydesigns.com/2014/04/my-parties-frozen-party-for-evite-and.html" target="_blank">
             GreyGrey Designs
            </a>
             Let it Go party inspired by the vibrant colors and bonds of sisterhood.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             The birthday girl has to look the part and luckily there are lots of options out there to make her feel special
            </strong>
           </p>
           <div class="figure_block size-100 aligncenter">
            <figure>
             <a href="http://communitytable.parade.com/308493/frozen3/">
              <img alt="" class="addthis_shareable at_include" data-parade-image="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/frozen3.png" data-parade-image-inlining="" data-parade-image-placeholding="true" src="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/themes/wp-theme/img/misc/tiny.gif"/>
             </a>
            </figure>
            <figcaption>
             <span class="arrow">
             </span>
             Credits from Left to Right
            </figcaption>
           </div>
           <p>
            1.
            <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Shawna-Brockmeier-Styled-Events/181564898529666" target="_blank">
             Shawna Brockmeier Styled Events
            </a>
            for Made by a Princess  You just cant top a custom handmade crown!
            <br/>
            2.
            <a href="https://www.etsy.com/shop/atutudes" target="_blank">
             Atutudes Hand Made Tutus
            </a>
             Each tutu is hand made with every detail perfectly executed.
            <br/>
            3. Signature character Elsa dress for the birthday girl and Elsa inspired t-shirt by
            <a href="http://www.partiesinstyle.com/" target="_blank">
             Made by a Princess
            </a>
            (Photo courtesy of
            <a href="http://www.flairedaffairs.com/" target="_blank">
             Flaired Affairs
            </a>
            from her daughters Frozen party).
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             I love unique touches in decorations
            </strong>
           </p>
           <div class="figure_block size-100 aligncenter">
            <figure>
             <a href="http://communitytable.parade.com/308494/frozen4/">
              <img alt="Credits from Left to Right " class="addthis_shareable at_include" data-parade-image="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/frozen4.png" data-parade-image-inlining="" data-parade-image-placeholding="true" src="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/themes/wp-theme/img/misc/tiny.gif"/>
             </a>
            </figure>
            <figcaption>
             <span class="arrow">
             </span>
             Credits from Left to Right
             <span class="credit">
              (Credits from Left to Right )
             </span>
            </figcaption>
           </div>
           <p>
            1.
            <a href="http://www.lillypauldesigns.com/" target="_blank">
             Lilly Paul Designs
            </a>
            for
            <a href="http://www.greygreydesigns.com/2014/04/my-parties-frozen-party-for-evite-and.html" target="_blank">
             GreyGrey Designs
            </a>
             Beautiful fabric garland matches the theme perfectly.
           </p>
           <p>
            2.
            <a href="http://catchmyparty.com/photos/1637006" target="_blank">
             Party Lab Miami
            </a>
             Hand painted wooden Elsa stand up is a stunning statement sure to wow guests.
           </p>
           <p>
            3.
            <a href="http://craftthatparty.blogspot.com/" target="_blank">
             Craft That Party
            </a>
            for
            <a href="http://www.greygreydesigns.com/2014/04/my-parties-frozen-party-for-evite-and.html" target="_blank">
             GreyGrey Design
            </a>
            s  Jenny Dixons peg dolls are little pieces of perfect artwork.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             Food is a huge part of any celebration
            </strong>
           </p>
           <div class="figure_block size-100 aligncenter">
            <figure>
             <a href="http://communitytable.parade.com/308499/frozen5/">
              <img alt="" class="addthis_shareable at_include" data-parade-image="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/frozen5.jpg" data-parade-image-inlining="" data-parade-image-placeholding="true" src="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/themes/wp-theme/img/misc/tiny.gif"/>
             </a>
            </figure>
            <figcaption>
             <span class="arrow">
             </span>
             Credits from Left to Right, by row.
            </figcaption>
           </div>
           <p>
            <span style="text-decoration: underline">
             Top Row
            </span>
           </p>
           <p>
            1.
            <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/She-Wears-The-Crown/383633378334432" target="_blank">
             She Wears the Crown
            </a>
            for
            <a href="http://www.madebyaprincessblog.com/2014/05/Frozen-Birthday-Party.html#axzz34HbU5uQ2" target="_blank">
             Made by a Princess
            </a>
             Gorgeous hand painted glitter Queen Megan cookies.
           </p>

              </script>

            </div>
           </div>
           <p>
            2.
            <a href="http://www.madebyaprincessblog.com/2014/05/Frozen-Birthday-Party.html#axzz34HbU5uQ2" target="_blank">
             Frost Berries
            </a>
             Fresh berries with a little tuft of blueberry cotton candy.
           </p>
           <p>
            3.
            <a href="http://www.madebyaprincessblog.com/2014/05/Frozen-Party-Food-Melted-Olaf-Recipe.html#axzz32Mx2nynr" target="_blank">
             Melted Olaf
            </a>
            - Greek yogurt with Olaf parts made to look like our favorite snowman is melting.
           </p>
           <p>
            <span style="text-decoration: underline">
             Middle Row
            </span>
           </p>
           <p>
            1.
            <a href="https://www.etsy.com/listing/183169083/snowflake-cupcake-toppers?ref=shop_home_active_11" target="_blank">
             Creativities Galore
            </a>
            for
            <a href="http://lauraslittlepartysite.blogspot.com/2014/03/frozen-dvd-kick-off-party.html" target="_blank">
             LAURAS little PARTY
            </a>
            - Custom toppers bring store bought cupcakes to life.
           </p>
           <p>
            2.
            <a href="http://www.evieandmallow.com/" target="_blank">
             Evie &amp; Mallow
            </a>
            for
            <a href="http://www.madebyaprincessblog.com/2014/05/Frozen-Birthday-Party.html#axzz34HbU5uQ2" target="_blank">
             Made by a Princess
            </a>
             Completely unique hand painted and glittered castle chocolates.
           </p>
           <p>
            3.
            <a href="https://www.facebook.com/101072046609448/photos/pb.101072046609448.-2207520000.1402462153./632572100126104/?type=3&amp;theater" target="_blank">
             4 Kids Cakes
            </a>
             Adorable and sparkly Elsa, Olaf, &amp; Anna inspired cake pops.
           </p>
           <p>
            <span style="text-decoration: underline">
             Bottom Row
            </span>
           </p>
           <p>
            1.
            <a href="https://www.facebook.com/SimplyaMayzingSweets" target="_blank">
             Simply aMAYzing Sweet
            </a>
            s for
            <a href="http://www.madebyaprincessblog.com/2014/05/Frozen-Birthday-Party.html#axzz34HbU5uQ2">
             Made by a Princess
            </a>
            - Snowflake and ice Rice Krispy treats capture the theme perfectly.
           </p>
           <p>
            2.
            <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Auntie-Beas-Bakery/123815327640548">
             Auntie Beas Bakery
            </a>
             Sparkly themed cookies fit for a princess!
           </p>
           <p>
            3.
            <a href="http://soiree-eventdesign.com/2014/01/frozen-party-ideas-ice-princess-party-printables/">
             Soiree Event Design
            </a>
             Custom cotton candy and coordinating themed labels add a special touch to the theme.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             Kids love activities so setting up activity stations is always a big hit and helps some of the shy kids ease into a new situation with people they may not know.
            </strong>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <div class="figure_block size-100 aligncenter">
            <figure>
             <a href="http://communitytable.parade.com/308500/frozen6/">
              <img alt="Credits from Left to Right " class="addthis_shareable at_include" data-parade-image="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/frozen6.jpg" data-parade-image-inlining="" data-parade-image-placeholding="true" src="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/themes/wp-theme/img/misc/tiny.gif"/>
             </a>
            </figure>
            <figcaption>
             <span class="arrow">
             </span>
             Credits from Left to Right
             <span class="credit">
              (Credits from Left to Right )
             </span>
            </figcaption>
           </div>
           <p>
            1.
            <a href="http://www.madebyaprincessblog.com/2014/05/Frozen-Birthday-Party.html#axzz34HbU5uQ2">
             Thaw Annas Frozen Heart
            </a>
             Kids had to melt the ice to free Annas frozen heart.
           </p>
           <p>
            2. Bubble Station by
            <a href="https://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=677760792281594&amp;set=a.397063670351309.90225.356267057764304&amp;type=1" target="_blank">
             Flaired Affairs
            </a>
             Each little girl had their own bubbles and princess wand.
           </p>
           <p>
            3.
            <a href="http://bethkruse.blogspot.com/2014/03/do-you-want-to-build-snowman.html">
             Do You Want to Build a Snowman
            </a>
            by Beth Kruse Custom Creations  Kids had fun creating their own snowman with cotton balls, stickers, and markers.
            <br/>
            <strong>
             Thank you to all of my friends for sharing their Frozen ideas with me! I hope you find some inspiration for your own celebrations.
            </strong>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <em>
             Photos for Made by a Princess courtesy of
             <a href="http://mariahealey.com/" target="_blank">

           </p>

           </p>
